First Draft's 3-0 Decklists
===========================



 Posted in **Event Coverage**
 on May 7, 2017 






![](https://media.magic.wizards.com/styles/auth_small/public/images/person/henke_author.jpg)
By Tobi Henke











With the eponymous Pro Tour next week featuring *Amonkhet* Booster Draft and with this weekend being the first outing of the set at Grand Prix events, information on the new format was at a premium. So how about we take a look at *all* the decks of the people who went 3-0 in the first draft at Grand Prix Bologna? Thanks to the judges who helped locating lists!


(Note that, because people played within draft pods but were paired based on overall record, draft tables could yield one, zero, or two 3-0 players.)







#### Francesco Giorgio, 3-0 in Draft Pod #1


##### 






![](https://web.archive.org/web/20160726232508im_/http://magic.wizards.com/sites/all/modules/features/wiz_bean_content_deck_list/icons/decklist_download.png)
